			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">Chipotle ANNOUNCES FIRST QUARTER 2022 RESULTS</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">Quarterly sales increase 16%,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;"> DRIVEN BY </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">9% </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">COMPARABLE restaurant SALES </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">GROWTH</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;border-bottom:1pt solid #996633 ;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#6E3F28;font-size:12pt;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">NEWPORT BEACH, Calf. &#x2013; April 26, 2022 &#x2013; Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) today reported financial results for its first quarter ended March 31, 2022.</font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Results for the three months ended </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">March</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">31</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">: &nbsp;</font>

		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Total r</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">evenue in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">first</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter was $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> billion, an increase of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">16.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">first</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1. The increase in total revenue was driven by a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">9.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% increase in comparable restaurant sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and new restaurant openings</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> Our </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">i</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">n-</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">r</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">estaurant sales increased 3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.1% in the three months ended March 31, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2022,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> as compared to the three months ended March 31, 2021, while digital sales represented 4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% of total </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">food and beverage revenue</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font>

These formats continue to perform very well and are helping enhance guest access and convenience, as well as increase new restaurant sa</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">les, margins, and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">returns. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Food, beverage and packaging costs in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">first</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter were 3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% of</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> total</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> revenue, a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">n</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">increase</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">00 basis points compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">first</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">crease was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">due to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">inflation across the menu, primarily due </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">to beef, avocados, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">paper,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> partially offset by leverage from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">menu price increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin was 2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">0.7</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">%, a </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">de</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">crease from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">22.3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">first</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">decrease was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">due to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">increases in hourly wages</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">higher </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">food </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">costs</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">partially </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">offset </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">by leverage from menu price increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and lower delivery expense</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;font-size:4pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;"> Restaurant level operating margin, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;">adjusted diluted earnings per share</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;">adjusted net income</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;">n</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;">on-GAAP general and administrative expenses, and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;">n</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;">on-GAAP effective income tax rate</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;font-size:8pt;"> are non-GAAP financial measures. Reconciliations to GAAP measures and further information are set forth in the table at the end of this press release.</font>

		</p>

Digital sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">include</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> revenue deferrals associated with Chipotle Rewards. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Conference Call Details</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">will</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> host a conference call on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Tuesday</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">April 26</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">2,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> at 4:30 PM Eastern time</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">discuss first quarter 2022 financial results as well as provide a business update for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">second quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">2022.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">conference</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> call can be accessed live over the phone by dialing 1-888-317-6003</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> or for international callers by dialing 1-412-317-6061</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> and use code: </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">5128212</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. The call will be webcast live from the company's website on the investor relations page at ir.chipotle.com/events. An archived webcast will be available approximately one hour after the end of the call.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About Chipotle</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) is cultivating a better world by serving responsibly sourced, classically-cooked, real food with wholesome ingredients without artificial colors, flavors or preservatives. Chipotle had </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">over</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3,000</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> restaurants as of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">March 31</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, in the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, France and Germany and is the only restaurant company of its size that owns and operates all its restaurants. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Chipotle is ranked on the Fortune 500 and is recognized on the 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> list for Fortune&#x2019;s Most Admired Companies. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">With </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">over</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">100</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">,000 em</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">ployees passionate about providing a great guest experience, Chipotle is a longtime leader and innovator in the fo</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">od industry. Chipotle is committed to making its food more accessible to everyone while continuing to be a brand with a demonstrated purpose as it leads the way in digital, technology and sustainable business practices. For more information or to place an order online, visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#C08C19;background-color: #FFFFFF;">WWW.CHIPOTLE.COM</font><font style="display: inline;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Forward-Looking Statements</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">Certain </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">statements in this press release are forward-looking statements as defined in the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, including statements about our goals for number of Chipotle restaurants, restaurants with Chipotlanes and rate of expansion,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">comparable restaurant sales, estimated tax rates, future cash flow, and future long-term prospects. We use words such as &#x201C;anticipate&#x201D;, &#x201C;believe&#x201D;, &#x201C;could&#x201D;, &#x201C;should&#x201D;, &#x201C;may&#x201D;, &#x201C;approximately&#x201D;, &#x201C;estimate&#x201D;, &#x201C;expect&#x201D;, &#x201C;potential&#x201D;, &#x201C;intend&#x201D;, &#x201C;project&#x201D;, &#x201C;encouraged&#x201D;, &#x201C;target&#x201D;, and similar terms and phrases, including references to assumptions, to identify forward-looking statements. The forward-looking statements in this press release are based on currently available operating, financial and competitive information available to us as of the date of this release and we assume no obligation to update these forward-looking statements. These statements are subject to risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from those described in the statements, including but not limited to: uncertainty regarding the duration and severity of the ongoing COVID-19 pandemic and its ultimate impact on our business, including supply chain disruptions and difficulties in acquiring restaurant equipment, impact on guest traffic, restaurant sales and operating costs and the ability of our third-party suppliers and business partners to fulfill their responsibilities and commitments; increasing wage inflation and the increasingly competitive labor market, which impacts our ability to attract and retain qualified employees and has resulted in occasional staffing shortages; increasing supply costs</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">(</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">including beef, avocados and paper</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">)</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">; risks associated with our reliance on certain information technology systems and potential failures or interruptions; privacy and cyber security risks related to our acceptance of electronic payments or electronic processing of confidential customer or employee information, including through our digital app; the impact of competition, including from sources outside the restaurant industry; the financial impact of increasing our national average hourly wage; the impact of federal, state or local government regulations relating to our employees, employment practices, restaurant design and construction, and the sale of food or alcoholic beverages; our ability to achieve our planned growth, such as the availability of suitable new restaurant sites and the availability of construction materials and contractors; increases in ingredient and other operating costs due to our Food With Integrity philosophy, tariffs or trade restrictions and supply shortages; the uncertainty of our ability to achieve expected levels of comparable restaurant sales due to factors such as changes in consumers' perceptions of our brand, including as a result of actual or rumored food safety concerns or other negative publicity, decreased overall consumer spending </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">(</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">cluding but not limited to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">the increase in inflation and higher gas prices</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">)</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> or the inability to increase menu prices or realize the benefits of menu price increases; risks associated with our increased focus on our digital business, including risks arising from our reliance on third party delivery services; risks relating to litigation, including possible governmental actions related to food safety incidents and potential class action litigation regarding employment laws, advertising claims or other matters; and other risk factors described from time to time in our SEC reports, including our annual report on Form 10-K and quarterly reports on Form 10-Q, all of which are available on the investor relations page of our website at ir.Chipotle.com. </font>

		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 3pt;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">RECONCILIATION OF NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES</font><font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="_Hlk22568764"></a><font style="display: inline;">The following tables provide a reconciliation of non-GAAP financial measures presented in the text above to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">Adjusted net income is net income excluding expenses related to </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">restaurant asset impairment, corporate restructuring, legal proceedings, stock-</font><font style="display: inline;">based compensation modification expense, and certain other costs. Adjusted general and administrative expense is general and administrative expense excluding transformation expenses, legal proceedings, stock-based compensation modification expense, and certain other costs. The adjusted effective income tax rate is the effective income tax rate adjusted to reflect the after tax impact of non-GAAP adjustments. Restaurant Level Operating Margin, a non-GAAP financial measure, is equal to the revenues generated by our restaurants less their direct operating costs which consist of food, beverage and packaging, labor, occupancy and other operating costs. This performance measure primarily includes the costs that restaurant level managers can directly control and excludes other operating costs that are essential to conduct our business. Management uses restaurant level operating margin as a measure of restaurant performance. Management believes restaurant level operating margin is useful to investors in that it highlights trends in our core business that may not otherwise be apparent to investors when relying solely on GAAP financial measures. We present these non-GAAP measures in order to facilitate meaningful evaluation of our operating performance across periods. These adjustments are intended to provide greater transparency of underlying performance and to allow investors to evaluate our business on the same basis as our management, which uses these non-GAAP measures in evaluating the company&#x2019;s performance. Our adjusted net income, adjusted diluted earnings per share, adjusted general and administrative expenses, adjusted effective income tax rate and restaurant level operating margin measures may not be comparable to other companies&#x2019; adjusted measures. These adjustments are not necessarily indicative of what our actual financial performance would have been during the periods presented and should be viewed in addition to, and not as an alternative to, our results prepared in accordance with GAAP. Further details regarding these adjustments are included in the tables below.</font>
		</p>
